Methodologies\nHealthgrades helps Americans find the right doctor for their unique needs by making profiles available for nearly every physician in America. Every doctor or other healthcare professional who has a listing with the National Professional Identifier Registry has a free profile on Healthgrades. Physicians can **[claim their free profile](https://update.healthgrades.com/?cid=22FAQ)** to add further detail including photos and care philosophy. There are advertising options available for hospitals or medical groups to promote their healthcare professionals on our site, and these profiles are clearly marked as sponsored profiles.\nRatings and Reviews\n\n...\n\n**Patient Satisfaction:** The doctor or other healthcare professional meets a minimum threshold for good patient ratings and reviews on Healthgrades.\n**Medical Sanctions:** The healthcare professional’s medical license has not been suspended, revoked, or surrendered. This data is updated twice a month.\nHealthgrades Choice™\nPatient Favorite\nHealthgrades is dedicated to providing transparent, high-quality insights to make searching for a healthcare provider more straightforward. The \"Patient Favorite\" badge reflects this commitment, serving as a beacon to help our users quickly and confidently identify top-performing providers.\nHere's what makes a provider a \"Patient Favorite\":\n1. Routine Care: Patient Favorite recognizes providers offering routine care, those who are often the first point of contact for patients. This includes family and internal physicians, dentists, psychiatrists, pediatricians, geriatricians, nurses, PAs, optometrists, and more.\n2. Patient Feedback:\n  1. The provider must have a star rating of 4.0 or higher.\n  2. The provider must have a minimum of 6 total reviews.\n  3. The provider must have received at least 5 written reviews in the past 5 years.\n3. License Integrity: Healthcare professionals must hold an active medical license free from sanctions or malpractice claims.\n\n...\n\nThe Healthgrades Patient Favorite designation is reserved for primary care doctors and healthcare professionals that have received exemplary patient ratings and reviews.\nThese individuals must have an aggregate rating of at least four (4) stars, a minimum of six (6) ratings with at least five (5) containing comments, all within the last five (5) years. Doctors and healthcare professionals can NOT pay or influence to receive the Patient Favorite badge.\n**What Healthgrades designation is better, Healthgrades Choice or Patient Favorite?**\nOne designation is not better than the other. They are both unique in their own way.\n\n...\n\nYou can opt-out of Healthgrades emails by visiting our secure email subscription manager [here](http://go.healthgrades.com/consumer-subscription-req) .\nDoes Healthgrades have an email newsletter?\nWe have a biweekly newsletter that covers a variety of health topics. You can sign up for this newsletter [here](http://go.healthgrades.com/newsletter-signup) . Healthgrades Search\nWhat is the \"Most Relevant\" sort option?\nWhen seeking a doctor on Healthgrades, you can search by name, specialty, condition, or procedure. You can further refine your search with filters including practice area, ratings, and insurance accepted. Sort options include closest, highest rated, and a proprietary “most relevant” sort.\nRelevance is determined by looking at a combination of experience, satisfaction ratings, hospital quality scores, distance, and appointment availability.\nWhat are \"Featured\" provider listings?\nFeatured listings on Healthgrades are a separate advertising product that allows profiles for doctors and other professionals from partner health systems and medical practices to appear as paid listings above the organic marketplace search results. These advertisements are clearly marked as “Featured.”\nAll featured profiles must still remain relevant to the search criteria to be shown in a paid slot. A healthcare professional’s participation or non-participation in Sponsored Results does not impact their ranking in the core marketplace search results. Note that doctors who are featured in the sponsored results will still appear in the organic search results.\nHow are \"Top Rated\" provider results determined?\nSome search results pages on Healthgrades.com may present \"Top Rated\" results, although many factors should be considered when choosing a provider, \"Top Rated\" results present only providers that have a 4-Star or above patient experience rating. Learn how factors like review volume, recency, and profile completeness affect rankings.\nWritten by\nEmily Manuel\nPublished\nOctober 8, 2025\n* Marketing\nShare:\n* Edited 2 months ago\n* Save Post\n\n...\n\n## Summarize with AI\nWhen patients search for a physician online, [Healthgrades](https://www.healthgrades.com/) is often one of the first sites they encounter. With more than 100 million visitors annually, it has become a trusted source for provider information and patient reviews, meaning that visibility on Healthgrades can have a direct impact on patient acquisition.\nSo, how exactly are doctors ranked on Healthgrades? While the platform doesn’t publish its full algorithm, there are several clear factors that determine how physicians appear in search results and how their profiles perform.\n\n## The Purpose of Healthgrades Rankings\nHealthgrades was designed to simplify provider selection by giving patients a **comparable, transparent look** at doctors’ backgrounds, specialties, and reputations. Rankings aren’t arbitrary; they’re meant to reflect both **clinical credibility** and **patient experience** .\nFor physicians, this means that, in addition to a medical degree, strong performance on Healthgrades requires consistent engagement and attention to online reputation.\n\n## Key Factors That Influence Rankings\n### 1. Review Volume and Quality\nThe single biggest driver of visibility on Healthgrades is **patient reviews** . Doctors with a higher number of reviews appear more prominently in search results than those with few or no reviews.\n* **Average star rating** matters, but **volume** is just as important. A physician with a 4.6-star rating across 150 reviews will often rank higher than a physician with a perfect 5-star score across only 6 reviews.\n* **Balanced feedback** (a mix of positive and negative reviews) is also valued by patients because it appears more authentic.\n\n...\n\n### 3. Profile Completeness\nHealthgrades gives preference to physicians with **fully completed profiles** , including:\n* A professional headshot.\n* Detailed biography highlighting education, specialties, and conditions treated.\n* Accepted insurance plans.\n* Languages spoken.\n* Affiliations with hospitals or health systems.\nThe more comprehensive and accurate the profile, the higher it tends to rank.\n\n...\n\n## Common Myths About Healthgrades Rankings\n### Myth #3: Star ratings are the only factor that matters.\nStar ratings are important, but without volume and recency, they don’t carry much weight. A perfect 5-star rating from 1 patient over a year ago will raise questions as to why there isn’t any recent feedback. Meanwhile, a 4.8-star rating across dozens of patients on a regular basis establishes credibility and trust, not just with patients, but also with Healthgrades and its algorithms.\n\n...\n\n## The Bottom Line\nDoctors are ranked on Healthgrades based on a combination of **patient feedback, profile completeness, and professional credibility** . While the exact algorithm is proprietary, the core principles driving visibility are clear: volume and recency of reviews, accurate and complete information, and active engagement.\nFor physicians and practices alike, the message is simple: **you can’t control the algorithm, but you** **_can_** **control your presence** . By consistently generating reviews, maintaining up-to-date profiles, and engaging with patients online, you ensure that your Healthgrades ranking reflects the quality of care you deliver every day.\nIn today’s digital-first healthcare environment, a strong Healthgrades presence isn’t optional — it’s a competitive necessity."],"source_id":"search_7f2ab8ba89054e5d8ef5765a74e9bb8f#6"},{"url":"https://resources.healthgrades.com/pro/video/healthgrades-101-video-library/where-healthgrades-gets-its-data","title":"Healthgrades 101 Video Library - Where Healthgrades Gets Its Data","publish_date":"2023-10-31","excerpts":["# Where Healthgrades Gets Its Data\nSpeaker 3Healthgrades data sources refresh as frequently as weekly and sometimes monthly, quarterly, or every six months. ## Learn more about Pediatricians and how to choose the right one for you

A pediatrician specializes in the physical, developmental, emotional and social health needs of children from birth to 21 years. Pediatricians provide infants, children and adolescents with a wide scope of care that includes comprehensive well-child care as well as prevention, diagnosis and treatment of acute and chronic diseases and injuries.

A pediatrician typically:

-   Examines the patient and evaluates their medical history
-   Provides primary healthcare services and immunizations
-   Provides health risk assessments and counseling
-   Diagnoses and treats acute and chronic diseases and conditions
-   Assesses growth and development
-   Orders and interprets laboratory and imaging tests and prescribes medications
-   Educates patients and their caretakers about wellness and disease prevention
-   Consults with other members of the patient’s medical team
-   Provides ongoing pediatric care in the doctor’s office, clinic and hospital

Pediatricians may also be known by the following names: pediatric physician, pediatric doctor, children’s doctor, primary care doctor, kids doctor, and primary care physician.

There are 117011 specialists practicing Pediatrics in San Jose, CA with an overall average rating of 4.1 stars. There are 4213 hospitals near San Jose, CA with affiliated Pediatrics specialists, including [Children's Hospital of Philadelphia](/hospital/childrens-hospital-of-philadelphia-b98951), [Boston Children's Hospital](/hospital/boston-childrens-hospital-f40a20) and [Cincinnati Children's Burney Campus](/hospital/cincinnati-childrens-burney-campus-5dee5a).

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA stay updated on the latest advancements and treatments in cardiovascular medicine?

Pediatrics Specialists have a variety of ways they stay current on the latest treatments and research within their specialty. These include subscribing to medical journals that publish peer-reviewed studies, attending in-person seminars or online webinars, or earning Continuing Medical Education (CME) credits to maintain their medical license.

During your appointment, ask your doctor or other healthcare professional about the ways they stay up-to-date about new treatments and how their learnings may affect your treatment options.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA collaborate with other healthcare providers to ensure comprehensive patient care?

Depending on your diagnosis and treatment plan, you may have a team of healthcare professionals working together to provide quality care.

In addition to your primary care physician and Pediatrics Specialist, you may consult with other specialists, physical therapists, speech therapists, nutritionists, psychologists, physician's assistants, and nurses, among many others. Together, your care team can address all facets of your care and collaborate on the most effective treatment plan for you.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA personalize treatment plans to meet the unique needs of each patient?

Your Pediatrics Specialist in CA will determine your individual treatment plan based on factors including your medical history, family history, lifestyle, cultural considerations, and personal preferences. Through honest communication, you and your doctor can work together to build a treatment plan that is tailored to you.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA approach holistic care, considering factors beyond just medical treatment?

In additional to your medical care, you may wish for your treatment plan to include complementary therapies that serve your physical, emotional, and spiritual well-being. These may include wellness practices such as acupuncture, massage, or yoga. You may seek mental health support through counselors, psychologists, and support groups. You might also find comfort in spiritual support from faith leaders and communities. Talk with your specialist about the types of therapies that will provide holistic benefits, and ask about any precautions to take to avoid potential interactions with your medical treatment.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA prioritize patient safety and infection control measures in their practice?

Patient safety, including prevention of healthcare-associated infections, is a priority of all healthcare professionals. Both within physician practices and in hospital settings, team members take precautions to protect patients' health and safety during their care. This includes thorough handwashing, sterilization of equipment, and routine cleaning of rooms and facilities.

The quality ratings of a physician's associated hospitals can also indicate a hospital's record for patient safety. A hospital with fewer healthcare-associated infections is likely to have better procedure outcomes, which will be reflected in higher quality ratings.

What resources are available to support patients in navigating insurance coverage and financial assistance with Pediatrics Specialists in CA?

Your Pediatrics Specialist's office can provide information about financial assistance, which may be referred to as charity care. Some doctor's offices also offer payment plans that allow you to pay your bill over a certain period of time.

If you need to receive care at a hospital, you may qualify for financial assistance through that hospital. If you receive care at a nonprofilt hospital, you must be offered financial assistance if you cannot afford to pay. If you participate in a government program, such as Medicaid or Medicare, those programs' websites can offer guidance about coverage for the care you need.

Your hospital may also have a patient advocate on staff who can help guide you through your coverage or your financial assistance options. You can also find a your own guide through the Patient Advocate Foundation.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA contribute to ongoing medical research and advancements in their field?

In addition to offering clincal care, many Pediatrics Specialists work outside of their practice in a variety of areas, including research, clinical trials, academic collaborations, or professional organizations. Through this work, Pediatrics Specialists can share their own research, learn about treatment advances, and bring innovative new therapies to their practices.

How do Pediatrics Specialists in CA accommodate patients with disabilities or special needs in their practice?

All patients have a right to accessible and equitable care, including those with disabilities or special needs. Healthcare facilities must adhere to the Americans with Disabilities Act (ADA) and offer a range of accommodations to ensure accessibility. These may include structural features, such as ramps or wide entrances; language services, such as translators or sign language interpreters; accessible signage for people with impaired vision; or exam rooms and medical equipment that can be used by people with mobility aids.

What measures do Pediatrics Specialists in CA take to ensure patient privacy and confidentiality in their practice?

Patient data protection and privacy rights are a top priority for all healthcare practices. The Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) requires healthcare professionals to follow established safeguards to protect private health information and imposes penalties for those who violate privacy rights. HIPAA also allows patients to understand exactly how their health information is used and decide with whom it may be shared.

Healthcare systems also have rigorous digital security protocols to protect electronic health records, and any staff members with access to health information receive training on privacy practices to maintain patient trust and confidentiality.

Pediatricians provide infants, children and adolescents with a wide scope of care that includes comprehensive well-child care as well as prevention, diagnosis and treatment of acute and chronic diseases and injuries.\nA pediatrician typically:\n* Examines the patient and evaluates their medical history\n* Provides primary healthcare services and immunizations\n* Provides health risk assessments and counseling\n* Diagnoses and treats acute and chronic diseases and conditions\n* Assesses growth and development\n* Orders and interprets laboratory and imaging tests and prescribes medications\n* Educates patients and their caretakers about wellness and disease prevention\n* Consults with other members of the patient’s medical team\n* Provides ongoing pediatric care in the doctor’s office, clinic and hospital\nPediatricians may also be known by the following names: pediatric physician, pediatric doctor, children’s doctor, primary care doctor, kids doctor, and primary care physician.\nThere are 2009 specialists practicing Pediatrics in Los Angeles, CA with an overall average rating of 4.1 stars. ## Learn more about Pediatrics Specialists and how to choose the right one for you

A pediatrician specializes in the physical, developmental, emotional and social health needs of children from birth to 21 years. Pediatricians provide infants, children and adolescents with a wide scope of care that includes comprehensive well-child care as well as prevention, diagnosis and treatment of acute and chronic diseases and injuries.

A pediatrician typically:

-   Examines the patient and evaluates their medical history
-   Provides primary healthcare services and immunizations
-   Provides health risk assessments and counseling
-   Diagnoses and treats acute and chronic diseases and conditions
-   Assesses growth and development
-   Orders and interprets laboratory and imaging tests and prescribes medications
-   Educates patients and their caretakers about wellness and disease prevention
-   Consults with other members of the patient’s medical team
-   Provides ongoing pediatric care in the doctor’s office, clinic and hospital

Pediatricians may also be known by the following names: pediatric physician, pediatric doctor, children’s doctor, primary care doctor, kids doctor, and primary care physician.

There are 4034 specialists practicing Pediatrics in Los Angeles, CA with an overall average rating of 4.1 stars.

## Dr. Belzer's Reviews
### Your trust is our top concern.
We strive to keep reviews honest, trustworthy, and fair.
Doctors can not pay for good reviews, nor can they pay to have negative reviews removed.
We monitor all reviews to ensure they comply with our guidelines and don’t include personal information, profanity, libel, defamation, harassment, obscenity or fraud.
Any reviews that are deemed fraudulent or violate our [guidelines](https://www.healthgrades.com/content/community-review-guidelines) will be removed immediately.
All reviews are confirmed and audited before publication, and community members have the ability to flag inappropriate content for further review by our team.

### Your trust is our top concern.

We strive to keep reviews honest, trustworthy, and fair.

Doctors can not pay for good reviews, nor can they pay to have negative reviews removed.

We monitor all reviews to ensure they comply with our guidelines and don’t include personal information, profanity, libel, defamation, harassment, obscenity or fraud.

Any reviews that are deemed fraudulent or violate our [guidelines](https://www.healthgrades.com/content/community-review-guidelines) will be removed immediately.

All reviews are confirmed and audited before publication, and community members have the ability to flag inappropriate content for further review by our team.

### Your trust is our top concern.

We strive to keep reviews honest, trustworthy, and fair.

Doctors can not pay for good reviews, nor can they pay to have negative reviews removed.

We monitor all reviews to ensure they comply with our guidelines and don’t include personal information, profanity, libel, defamation, harassment, obscenity or fraud.

Any reviews that are deemed fraudulent or violate our [guidelines](https://www.healthgrades.com/content/community-review-guidelines) will be removed immediately.

All reviews are confirmed and audited before publication, and community members have the ability to flag inappropriate content for further review by our team.

## Frequently Asked Questions

How can I make a same-day appointment with a Pediatric Medicine Specialist in CA?

On average, patients who use Healthgrades can search for a Pediatric Medicine Specialist in CA, book an appointment, and see the Pediatric Medicine Specialist within 24 hours. Same-day appointments are often available, you can search for real-time availability of Specialists in CA who accept your insurance and make an appointment online.

How can I find a CA Pediatric Medicine Specialist who takes my insurance?

Healthgrades lets you search specifically for a CA Pediatric Medicine Specialist who takes your insurance. Just choose your carrier and plan from the drop-down menu at the top of the page. If you’re not sure which plan you have, you can use Healthgrades’s insurance checker to find out.

How can I find a female Pediatric Medicine Specialist in CA?

When you search for CA Specialists on Healthgrades, you can filter your results by gender, in addition to other criteria. That way, you’ll only see Specialists in CA who match your preferences.

How can I book an appointment online with a Pediatric Medicine Specialist in CA?

Healthgrades provides appointment information for all Specialists in CA. You can search for CA Specialists by symptom or visit reason. Then, choose your insurance plan. Based on that information, you’ll see a list of providers who meet your search criteria, along with their available appointment slots.

How can I find a CA Pediatric Medicine Specialist who sees patients after hours?

On Healthgrades, you can search specifically for CA Specialists with availability after 5 p.m.

How can I find a top-rated Pediatric Medicine Specialist in CA?

You can use Healthgrades to find Specialists in CA who are highly rated by other patients. These ratings are based on verified reviews submitted by real patients. Every time a patient completes an appointment booked on Healthgrades, they’re invited to review their experience. Each review must comply with Healthgrades’s guidelines.

Dr. Diane Tanaka, MD is a pediatric medicine specialist in Los Angeles, CA and has over 35 years of experience in the medical field. ### Your trust is our top concern.

We strive to keep reviews honest, trustworthy, and fair.

Doctors can not pay for good reviews, nor can they pay to have negative reviews removed.

We monitor all reviews to ensure they comply with our guidelines and don’t include personal information, profanity, libel, defamation, harassment, obscenity or fraud.

Any reviews that are deemed fraudulent or violate our [guidelines](https://www.healthgrades.com/content/community-review-guidelines) will be removed immediately.

All reviews are confirmed and audited before publication, and community members have the ability to flag inappropriate content for further review by our team.

# Dr. Tracey Norton, DO

## Pediatric Medicine | 45+ years of experience

45+ years of experience

5 Star Rating

Based on 1 review 5.0 Star Rating (1 review)

ReviewSave

Dr. Tracey Norton, DO is a pediatric medicine specialist in Los Angeles, CA and has over 45 years of experience in the medical field. She graduated from A. T. Still University Kirksville College of Osteopathic Medicine in 1978. She is accepting new patients and telehealth appointments.

5 Star Rating

Based on 1 review 5.0 Star Rating (1 review)

## About Me

### biography

Dr. Tracey Norton, DO is a pediatric medicine specialist in Los Angeles, CA and has over 45 years of experience in the medical field. She graduated from A. T. Still University Kirksville College of Osteopathic Medicine in 1978. She is accepting new patients and telehealth appointments.
